  <script>
   wbq.push(function manageHamburgerMenu() {
  var $nav = $('.js__nav');
  var $navCloseBtn = $('#nav-close-btn');
  var $navToggleBtn = $('.js__btn--nav-toggle');

  function lockNavFocus() {
    $navCloseBtn.focus();
    document.addEventListener('focusin', focusNavCloseBtn);
  }

  function focusNavCloseBtn(event) {
    if (!$.contains(document.getElementById('masthead-nav'), event.target)) {
      $navCloseBtn.focus();
    }
  }

  function unlockNavFocus() {
    document.removeEventListener('focusin', focusNavCloseBtn);
    $navToggleBtn.focus();
  }

  // hamburger menu to toggle mobile nav, full screen hit area beneath
  // mobile nav to act as toggle target
  $navToggleBtn.click(function (event) {
    $nav.toggleClass('nav--is-open');
    if ($nav.hasClass('nav--is-open')) {
      if (window.DEVICE_VIEW === 'desktop') {
        lockNavFocus();
      }
      window.TMZ.utils.setAccessibilityFocusTrap('masthead-nav');
      $nav.css('visibility', 'visible');
    } else {
      window.TMZ.utils.removeAccessibilityFocusTrap();
      if (window.DEVICE_VIEW === 'desktop') {
        unlockNavFocus();
        $navToggleBtn.focus();
      }
      setTimeout(function () {
        $nav.css('visibility', 'hidden');
      }, 300);
    }

    event.preventDefault();
  });
});
  </script>
  <!--/.nav-->

  <script>
   wbq.push(function manageTipMenu() {
  var $tip = $('.js__tip');
  var $tipCloseBtn = $('#tip__btn-close');
  var $tipToggleBtn = $('.js__btn--tip-toggle');
  var $nav = $('.js__nav');

  function lockTipFocus() {
    $tipCloseBtn.focus();
    document.addEventListener('focusin', focusTipCloseBtn);
  }

  function focusTipCloseBtn(event) {
    if (!$.contains(document.getElementById('tip'), event.target)) {
      $tipCloseBtn.focus();
    }
  }

  function unlockTipFocus() {
    document.removeEventListener('focusin', focusTipCloseBtn);
  }

  // toggle tip full screen mobile menu
  $tipToggleBtn.click(function (event) {
    $tip.toggleClass('tip--is-open');
    if ($tip.hasClass('tip--is-open')) {
      if (window.DEVICE_VIEW === 'desktop') {
        lockTipFocus();
      }
      window.TMZ.utils.setAccessibilityFocusTrap('tip');
      $tip.css('visibility', 'visible');
      setTimeout(function() {
        $nav.css('visibility', 'hidden');
      }, 300);
    } else {
      window.TMZ.utils.removeAccessibilityFocusTrap();
      if (window.DEVICE_VIEW === 'desktop') {
        unlockTipFocus();
        $tipToggleBtn.focus();
      }
      setTimeout(function() {
        $tip.css('visibility', 'hidden');
      }, 300);
    }

    // Hide nav
    if ($nav.hasClass('nav--is-open')) {
      setTimeout(function () {
        $nav.removeClass('nav--is-open');
      }, 300);
    }
    event.preventDefault();
  });
});
  </script>

         <script>
          wbq.push(function renderVideoBlock() {
        var page = window.TMZ.select(window.TMZ.selectors.getPage);
        // there is a weird bug with iPhone 6+ on iOS 9.3.4 where the spinner gets revealed even after its
        // event listener has been removed, so for now this stupid flag can correct for that.
        var isResolved = false;
        if (!page.isTurbolinksPreview) {
          function displayPlayer(player) {
            if (player.id === 'jwplayer-video-player-8f7f7e8b-29bc-493f-a104-bff8cbbcd3ce-547022354-player') {
              player.getContainer().closest('.embed-responsive-item--jwplayer').classList.remove('invisible');
              return;
            }
            // a fallback video
            player.closest('.embed-responsive-item--jwplayer').classList.remove('invisible');
          }
          function fadeImageHolderAndFooter() {
            var imageHolder = document.getElementById('video-player-8f7f7e8b-29bc-493f-a104-bff8cbbcd3ce-547022354-image-holder');
            var footer = document.getElementById('video-player-8f7f7e8b-29bc-493f-a104-bff8cbbcd3ce-547022354-footer');
            if (imageHolder) {
              imageHolder.addEventListener('transitionend', removeImageHolder, { once: true });
              imageHolder.classList.add('video-block__image-holder-fade');
            }

            if (footer && !footer.classList.contains('hidden')) {
              footer.addEventListener('transitionend', removeFooter, { once: true });
              footer.classList.add('video-block__media-footer-fade');
            }
          }
          function removeImageHolder() {
            var imageHolder = document.getElementById('video-player-8f7f7e8b-29bc-493f-a104-bff8cbbcd3ce-547022354-image-holder');
            if (imageHolder) {
              imageHolder.remove();
            }
          }
          function removeFooter() {
            var footer = document.getElementById('video-player-8f7f7e8b-29bc-493f-a104-bff8cbbcd3ce-547022354-footer');
            if (footer) {
              footer.classList.add('hidden');
            }
          }
          function hideSpinner() {
            var spinner = document.getElementById('video-player-8f7f7e8b-29bc-493f-a104-bff8cbbcd3ce-547022354-progress-spinner');
            spinner.classList.add('below');
            spinner.classList.remove('above');
          }
          function revealSpinner() {
            if (isResolved) {
              return;
            }
            var spinner = document.getElementById('video-player-8f7f7e8b-29bc-493f-a104-bff8cbbcd3ce-547022354-progress-spinner');
            spinner.classList.add('above');
            spinner.classList.remove('below');
          }
          window.TMZ.videos.observe(document.getElementById('jwplayer-video-player-8f7f7e8b-29bc-493f-a104-bff8cbbcd3ce-547022354'), {
                        onObserve: function() {
              document.getElementById('video-player-8f7f7e8b-29bc-493f-a104-bff8cbbcd3ce-547022354-play-btn').addEventListener('mousemove', revealSpinner, { once: true });
            },
            onResolve: function(player) {
              isResolved = true;
              var playButton = document.getElementById('video-player-8f7f7e8b-29bc-493f-a104-bff8cbbcd3ce-547022354-play-btn');
              playButton.removeEventListener('mousemove', revealSpinner);
              playButton.addEventListener('click', function() {
                displayPlayer(player);
                player.play();
                removeImageHolder();
                removeFooter();
                window.TMZ.dispatch(window.TMZ.actions.clickLink(
                  'https://www.tmz.com/videos/2021-03-08-030721-meghan-markle-archie-1051458/',
                  null,
                  'tmz:video:8f7f7e8b-29bc-493f-a104-bff8cbbcd3ce',
                  null,
                  {
                    section: 'blogroll',
                    name: 'video',
                    action: 'click'
                  }
                ));
              }, { once: true });
              hideSpinner();
            }
                      });
        }
      });
         </script>

        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-7500ad365106373d8aefc98a6363b0f1">
         <p>
          Meghan also said she was silenced by the Firm, which manages Royal business, but given assurances she would be protected. Meghan then said they never protected her, saying ... "They were willing to lie to protect other members, but not willing to tell the truth about me."
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-7500ad365106373d8aefc98a6363b0f1-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-b5ea5fa02e03d1323a2d0fa11a060d08">
         <p>
          Prince Harry eventually came on and corroborated Meg's claim that somebody brought up race as it pertained to their child, Archie, and even elaborated ... saying it was brought up early and often.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-b5ea5fa02e03d1323a2d0fa11a060d08-->

Basically, he's taking that to the grave -- but he did say this ... it was clear from the get-go with Meghan that race was something that was on the Royal Family's mind, and that it was going to be difficult to navigate.

        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-image-block canvas-image-block-blogroll canvas-image-block--default canvas-block-is-first" id="cb-921eb63b6e42abb67867a7f8481eb300">
         <div class="image-block">
          <img alt="" class="img-fluid image-block__img-fluid img-aspect-auto" loading="lazy" src="https://imagez.tmz.com/image/f7/4by3/2021/03/08/f7863ad62a744c879d916c9993dd3292_md.jpg"/>

        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-98454ab5c52d57ac69bfbbc124d6c0df">
         <p>
          Pepe Le Pew's problematic behavior appears to have been something Warner Bros. was well aware of before he was called out anew ... because he reportedly doesn't make a single appearance in the new 'Space Jam.'
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-98454ab5c52d57ac69bfbbc124d6c0df-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-76ad85d8b244f3ab288a8cdce55a6f1d">
         <p>
          A new
          <a href="https://deadline.com/2021/03/pepe-le-pew-space-jam-2-new-york-times-rape-culture-controversy-1234708688/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
           <strong>
            Deadline
           </strong>
          </a>
          report explains that the Looney Tunes character actually had a scene written into the movie early on in the production, when director
          <strong>
           Terence Nance
          </strong>
          was still at the helm. Apparently, there was a 'Casablanca'-like scene in which Pepe played a bartender and tried kissing the arm of a human character, portrayed by actress
          <strong>
           Greice Santo
          </strong>
          .
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-76ad85d8b244f3ab288a8cdce55a6f1d-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-image-block canvas-image-block-blogroll canvas-image-block--default" id="cb-66f6cdbaf0dea5404a3cc95dd543723c">
         <div class="image-block">
          <img alt="" class="img-fluid image-block__img-fluid img-aspect-auto" loading="lazy" src="https://imagez.tmz.com/image/7f/4by3/2021/03/08/7f69b15c548d4296a1bf740bbdddc471_md.jpg"/>
         </div>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-66f6cdbaf0dea5404a3cc95dd543723c-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-ce360d120fe001b57760d614f4afbe46">
         <p>
          Deadline says Santo pulls back and slapped Pepe silly ... and
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/people/lebron-james/">
           <strong>
            LeBron James
           </strong>
          </a>
          actually gave him a pep talk of sorts, letting him know it wasn't cool to get grabby without consent. The outlet also says Pepe referenced his longtime muse, Penelope Pussycat, and said she'd taken out a restraining order against him ... at least that's what was going to be in the flick before it was scrapped when
          <strong>
           Malcolm D. Lee
          </strong>
          took over as director.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-ce360d120fe001b57760d614f4afbe46-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-d484ff6da436038a4ee7f6e8dc62f810">
         <p>
          Word is, the Pepe scene was axed entirely in the final cut of the film -- which is set to debut this summer -- and according to folks who've seen a screening of the movie, per Deadline, they say there's no trace of Pepe anywhere in what people will see on HBO Max.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-d484ff6da436038a4ee7f6e8dc62f810-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-youtube-video-block canvas-youtube-video-block-blogroll canvas-youtube-video-block--default" id="cb-344af9357cbf4e5e1189689f2ff37993">
         <div class="d-flex justify-content-center" id="cb-344af9357cbf4e5e1189689f2ff37993-1264295631-target">

      function styleIframe(e) {
        var iframe = e.target.getIframe();
        iframe.classList.add('embed-responsive');
        if (!iframe.getAttribute('width')) {
          iframe.setAttribute('width', targetWidth);
        }
        if (!iframe.getAttribute('height')) {
          iframe.setAttribute('height', targetWidth / (16 / 9));
        }
      }

              window.TMZ.utils.loadYouTubeJs()
          .then(function initYouTubeBlock() {
            initPlayer(function onReady(e) {
              styleIframe(e);
              cueVideo(e);
                                        });
          }).catch(fail);
          });
         </script>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-6a3b19c65aeaed23b58acff2dc80fce9-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-983c01b2fce842f7cc8e6cc30a87ed66">
         <p>
          In response, LeBron said this about his own decision on the vaccine ... "That's a conversation that, you know, my family and I will have. And, probably pretty much keep that to a private thing." He said he was aware of Silver's comments, but insisted it was something to be discussed among the family and not in public, and that's where he was going to keep it.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-983c01b2fce842f7cc8e6cc30a87ed66-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-a614e9a6d163cd0d19d781a83b4fc0ad">
         <p>
          That's fascinating, considering LeBron is by far one of the most influential people in the world ... and perhaps the second or third most influential African-American. The fact he's wishy-washy on whether he'll get it speaks volumes, and could well influence others in the community.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-a614e9a6d163cd0d19d781a83b4fc0ad-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-image-block canvas-image-block-blogroll canvas-image-block--default" id="cb-43226db9cb55bac60d62fd7fb50bda66">
         <div class="image-block">
          <img alt="" class="img-fluid image-block__img-fluid img-aspect-auto" loading="lazy" src="https://imagez.tmz.com/image/09/4by3/2021/03/07/099e694114334c858de3816ced20c789_md.jpg"/>
          <div class="image-block__card-footer">
           <span class="media-credit image-block__media-credit">
            Shutterstock Premier
           </span>
          </div>
         </div>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-43226db9cb55bac60d62fd7fb50bda66-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-d6f7202bd582a5300b1aa32b07d10d85">
         <p>
          Of course, vaccinations have been a major issue in the Black community ... as many simply don't trust it -- due to a number of historical atrocities perpetuated onto African-Americans and other factors as well. But, many prominent Black role models have been trying to convince the Black community this vaccine is safe and worth taking ... like the late, great
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/people/hank-aaron/">
           <strong>
            Hank Aaron
           </strong>
          </a>
          .
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-d6f7202bd582a5300b1aa32b07d10d85-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default canvas-block-is-last" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-2decd364f47e492b31ab5cc550665eca">
         <p>
          Before he
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/2021/01/22/hank-aaron-dead-died-baseball-legend/">
           <strong>
            passed away
           </strong>
          </a>
          in late January, Aaron made a point
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/2021/01/05/hank-aaron-covid-vaccine-morehouse/">
           <strong>
            to get the vaccine
           </strong>
          </a>
          and to do so publicly, as he wanted to put out the right message and have Black Americans follow suit. He said, in part ... "I feel quite proud of myself for doing something like this. ... Its just a small thing that can help zillions of people in this country." LeBron feels differently, it seems.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-2decd364f47e492b31ab5cc550665eca-->
       </div>

       <header class="article__header">
        <a class="article__header-link js-track-link" data-context='{"section":"main","name":"headline","pos":4}' data-node-ref="tmz:article:ee8da126-e35e-4157-9b1d-39e3e0fc528a" data-widget-ref="tmz:blogroll-widget:39cc321d-66b9-57e0-816e-f745a6fcb489" href="https://www.tmz.com/2021/03/07/bethenny-frankel-mocks-meghan-markle-plight-oprah-interview/">
         <h2 class="article__header-title">
          <span class="article__hf1 text-uppercase h3">
           Bethenny Frankel
          </span>
          <span class="article__hf2 text-uppercase h1">
           Blasts Meghan Markle's 'Plight'
          </span>
          <span class="article__hf3 text-none h2">
           ... Hours Before Oprah Tell-All
          </span>
         </h2>
        </a>
        <h5 class="article__published-at">
         <ul class="social social--sm">
          <li class="social-item">
           <a aria-label="Share on Facebook" class="btn social__btn social__btn--sm social__btn--facebook js-track-link" data-context='{"section":"main","name":"facebook-header","pos":4}' data-node-ref="tmz:article:ee8da126-e35e-4157-9b1d-39e3e0fc528a" data-widget-ref="tmz:blogroll-widget:39cc321d-66b9-57e0-816e-f745a6fcb489" href="https://www.tmz.com/2021/03/07/bethenny-frankel-mocks-meghan-markle-plight-oprah-interview/" onclick="window.open('http://www.facebook.com/sharer.php?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.tmz.com%2F2021%2F03%2F07%2Fbethenny-frankel-mocks-meghan-markle-plight-oprah-interview%2F', '_blank', 'status=0,width=575,height=450');return false;">

         3/7/2021 12:29 PM PT
        </h5>
        <!--/.article__posted-date-->

       <div class="article__blocks">
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-image-block canvas-image-block-blogroll canvas-image-block--default canvas-block-is-first" id="cb-2d35297c110c142279cb861e6ee2c707">
         <div class="image-block">
          <img alt="" class="img-fluid image-block__img-fluid img-aspect-auto" loading="lazy" src="https://imagez.tmz.com/image/1a/4by3/2021/03/07/1aa416dd30c84ffa9f7833cff8cad06d_md.jpg"/>
          <div class="image-block__card-footer">
           <span class="media-credit image-block__media-credit">
            TMZ/Getty Composite
           </span>
          </div>
         </div>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-2d35297c110c142279cb861e6ee2c707-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-97c6bbd57cc05f0c360a201442270de2">
         <p>
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/people/meghan-markle/">
           <strong>
            Meghan Markle
           </strong>
          </a>
          's struggles adjusting to Royal life are getting ZERO sympathy from someone in the 'Real Housewives' world ... that'd be
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/people/bethenny-frankel/">
           <strong>
            Bethenny Frankel
           </strong>
          </a>
          , who's got choice words for the Duchess.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-97c6bbd57cc05f0c360a201442270de2-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-a2d28597a0390e2914060057b6f0140d">
         <p>
          The 'RHONY' star absolutely shredded Meghan Sunday just hours before her tell-all interview with
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/people/oprah-winfrey/">
           <strong>
            Oprah
           </strong>
          </a>
          was set to air on CBS ... invoking
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/people/justin-timberlake/">
           <strong>
            Justin Timberlake
           </strong>
          </a>
          in telling her to take her woe-is-me moment and basically shove it.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-a2d28597a0390e2914060057b6f0140d-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-image-block canvas-image-block-blogroll canvas-image-block--default" id="cb-5fd164ad4422a2f0565dc466d9d81d14">
         <div class="image-block">
          <img alt="" class="img-fluid image-block__img-fluid img-aspect-auto" loading="lazy" src="https://imagez.tmz.com/image/9e/4by3/2021/03/07/9efbd02496b04bdca0f308281d257252_md.jpg"/>
         </div>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-5fd164ad4422a2f0565dc466d9d81d14-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-5d11d9c87799fcbbb95a5a874f688c18">
         <p>
          Bethenny writes, "Cry me a river...the plight of being a game show host, fairly unknown actress, to suffering in a palace, w tiaras &amp; 7 figure weddings for TWO WHOLE YEARS to being a household name w @Oprah on speed dial, fetching 7 m for interviews, hundreds of millions in media deals. Thinking face #MARRY"
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-5d11d9c87799fcbbb95a5a874f688c18-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-742ea24e6c7c5d011f50a2cb5ab99f24">
         <p>
          On Saturday, Bethenny aired out even more of her grievances over the
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/2021/03/01/oprah-interview-prince-harry-meghan-markle-shocking-bombshell/">
           <strong>
            coverage the interview
           </strong>
          </a>
          was getting ... saying, "Not since @MonicaLewinsky interview, have people been obsessed with a young female interview like this #MARRY interview. Remember the famous lip gloss?"
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-742ea24e6c7c5d011f50a2cb5ab99f24-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-image-block canvas-image-block-blogroll canvas-image-block--default" id="cb-b83673e8eea2919d77f6c545e0901b52">
         <div class="image-block">
          <img alt="" class="img-fluid image-block__img-fluid img-aspect-auto" loading="lazy" src="https://imagez.tmz.com/image/c7/4by3/2021/03/07/c70836813e85458d90325d5a5b72bce1_md.jpg"/>
         </div>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-b83673e8eea2919d77f6c545e0901b52-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-0d3e268848aaf7f0d10295ed843a8c68">
         <p>
          Someone replied to her with a collage of headlines past about how her staff had reportedly been
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/2021/03/04/meghan-markle-prince-harry-oprah-interview-lies-buckingham-palace-the-firm/">
           <strong>
            catty towards her
           </strong>
          </a>
          right out the gate ... and that's what set Bethenny off anew.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-0d3e268848aaf7f0d10295ed843a8c68-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-2f18e0a0145dc92ca8d970c3cf4d572d">
         <p>
          She continued with her tirade, going on to say she gives
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/people/prince-harry/">
           <strong>
            Harry
           </strong>
          </a>
          a break here -- as she doesn't feel he's the one pulling the strings for all this press the couple is now receiving ... something he's repeatedly said he's not a big fan of in light of what happened to his mother,
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/people/princess-diana/">
           <strong>
            Diana
           </strong>
          </a>
          .
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-2f18e0a0145dc92ca8d970c3cf4d572d-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-twitter-tweet-block canvas-twitter-tweet-block-blogroll canvas-twitter-tweet-block--default" id="cb-c6c400c8383cd876257b4feb8152a25f">
         <div class="d-flex justify-content-center" id="cb-c6c400c8383cd876257b4feb8152a25f-270971984-target">
          <blockquote class="twitter-tweet">
           <p dir="ltr" lang="en">
            I chose reality tv, to work towards making $, to be scrutinized &amp; criticized.I took the trappings &amp; the beatings along with it. Its a rose w petals &amp; thorns. People beg to enter the often toxic institution I signed up for. That WAS the life I chose. You cant play stupid &amp; smart
           </p>
            Bethenny Frankel (@Bethenny)
           <a href="https://twitter.com/Bethenny/status/1368580668624674820?ref_src=twsrc^tfw">
            March 7, 2021
           </a>
           <a href="https://twitter.com/Bethenny" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
            @Bethenny
           </a>
          </blockquote>
         </div>

      });
    }).catch(reject);

    // there is no "accepted" html for twitter block, the above js does it all

});
         </script>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-c6c400c8383cd876257b4feb8152a25f-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-81071c9efc5ac65ec106eced34e91599">
         <p>
          BF ended her thoughts with one last apparent shot at Meghan, writing ... "I chose reality tv, to work towards making $, to be scrutinized &amp; criticized. I took the trappings &amp; the beatings along with it. Its a rose w petals &amp; thorns. People beg to enter the often toxic institution I signed up for. That WAS the life I chose. You cant play stupid &amp; smart."
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-81071c9efc5ac65ec106eced34e91599-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default canvas-block-is-last" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-12807b4657a540d4849dfe48f4c76b0a">
         <p>
          Tell us how you really feel, Beth.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-12807b4657a540d4849dfe48f4c76b0a-->

         <p>
          <strong class="updated-time--strong">
           2:39 PM PT
          </strong>
          -- Scottsdale PD tells TMZ ... two women were criminally charged in connection to this incident, but wouldn't say which ones or what the charges were.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-e6e2db9e4812e89a8bf0405dcfa2fbcc-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default updated" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-864a8179a568a4b35b86d824f9a3a006">
         <p>
          We're told a preliminary investigation shows the whole thing started because somebody cut in line, and SPD insists this had nothing to do with race or mask-wearing.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-864a8179a568a4b35b86d824f9a3a006-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-2ffc1f6fae3fe4be6bd1f4aa2225f753">
         <p>
          A brawl broke out at a Bath &amp; Body Works in Arizona, where the employees of all people are the ones who stepped in ... and proceeded to whoop on a woman.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-2ffc1f6fae3fe4be6bd1f4aa2225f753-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-e4c6a51c0a7b0faedbffa8179ddc4e1d">
         <p>
          Check out this insane fight that broke out over the weekend at the Fashion Square Mall in Scottsdale -- where a middle-aged woman is said to have been causing a ruckus inside with another customer before s*** hit the fan.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-e4c6a51c0a7b0faedbffa8179ddc4e1d-->

          The person who shot this claims the lady was standing too close to another customer and they started arguing ... something she says the workers tried deescalating.
         </p>

        <!--/#cb-c871220bfbc36f71a6cbfb4d7a337514-->

         <p>
          At some point, somebody put hands on the other ... and all hell broke loose. You see an employee start to go at it with the blonde woman, while her co-worker rushes over to help ... knocking everyone over in the process. Not too far away, another woman gets into it with yet another worker.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-9a1d17c49528c517171bdf1ba1ad1068-->

         <p>
          Eventually, a male employee steps in to break it up -- and he orders the women who were fighting to get the heck out of their establishment. The blonde lady tells him to stop touching her, and then says she ain't leaving 'til she can get her purse amid the commotion.
         </p>
        </section>

         <script>
          wbq.push(function renderVideoBlock() {
        var page = window.TMZ.select(window.TMZ.selectors.getPage);
        // there is a weird bug with iPhone 6+ on iOS 9.3.4 where the spinner gets revealed even after its
        // event listener has been removed, so for now this stupid flag can correct for that.
        var isResolved = false;
        if (!page.isTurbolinksPreview) {
          function displayPlayer(player) {
            if (player.id === 'jwplayer-video-player-f16dfbca-6639-48d6-9b73-52a36c4027d8-579272523-player') {
              player.getContainer().closest('.embed-responsive-item--jwplayer').classList.remove('invisible');
              return;
            }
            // a fallback video
            player.closest('.embed-responsive-item--jwplayer').classList.remove('invisible');
          }
          function fadeImageHolderAndFooter() {
            var imageHolder = document.getElementById('video-player-f16dfbca-6639-48d6-9b73-52a36c4027d8-579272523-image-holder');
            var footer = document.getElementById('video-player-f16dfbca-6639-48d6-9b73-52a36c4027d8-579272523-footer');
            if (imageHolder) {
              imageHolder.addEventListener('transitionend', removeImageHolder, { once: true });
              imageHolder.classList.add('video-block__image-holder-fade');
            }

            if (footer && !footer.classList.contains('hidden')) {
              footer.addEventListener('transitionend', removeFooter, { once: true });
              footer.classList.add('video-block__media-footer-fade');
            }
          }
          function removeImageHolder() {
            var imageHolder = document.getElementById('video-player-f16dfbca-6639-48d6-9b73-52a36c4027d8-579272523-image-holder');
            if (imageHolder) {
              imageHolder.remove();
            }
          }
          function removeFooter() {
            var footer = document.getElementById('video-player-f16dfbca-6639-48d6-9b73-52a36c4027d8-579272523-footer');
            if (footer) {
              footer.classList.add('hidden');
            }
          }
          function hideSpinner() {
            var spinner = document.getElementById('video-player-f16dfbca-6639-48d6-9b73-52a36c4027d8-579272523-progress-spinner');
            spinner.classList.add('below');
            spinner.classList.remove('above');
          }
          function revealSpinner() {
            if (isResolved) {
              return;
            }
            var spinner = document.getElementById('video-player-f16dfbca-6639-48d6-9b73-52a36c4027d8-579272523-progress-spinner');
            spinner.classList.add('above');
            spinner.classList.remove('below');
          }
          window.TMZ.videos.observe(document.getElementById('jwplayer-video-player-f16dfbca-6639-48d6-9b73-52a36c4027d8-579272523'), {
                        onObserve: function() {
              document.getElementById('video-player-f16dfbca-6639-48d6-9b73-52a36c4027d8-579272523-play-btn').addEventListener('mousemove', revealSpinner, { once: true });
            },
            onResolve: function(player) {
              isResolved = true;
              var playButton = document.getElementById('video-player-f16dfbca-6639-48d6-9b73-52a36c4027d8-579272523-play-btn');
              playButton.removeEventListener('mousemove', revealSpinner);
              playButton.addEventListener('click', function() {
                displayPlayer(player);
                player.play();
                removeImageHolder();
                removeFooter();
                window.TMZ.dispatch(window.TMZ.actions.clickLink(
                  'https://www.tmz.com/videos/2021-03-07-030721-jerry-springer-1051447/',
                  null,
                  'tmz:video:f16dfbca-6639-48d6-9b73-52a36c4027d8',
                  null,
                  {
                    section: 'blogroll',
                    name: 'video',
                    action: 'click'
                  }
                ));
              }, { once: true });
              hideSpinner();
            }
                      });
        }
      });

        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-ea08b853b1530a5d12d20aea716879b1">
         <p>
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/people/jerry-springer/">
           <strong>
            Jerry Springer
           </strong>
          </a>
          revisited his pre-pandemic tradition of singing a famous
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/people/elvis-presley/">
           <strong>
            Elvis
           </strong>
          </a>
          tune for the King's birthday -- albeit a couple months late ... but still as incredible as ever.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-ea08b853b1530a5d12d20aea716879b1-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-8673c67c80b7b0685e3e6ba7e6f8db41">
         <p>
          The famed talk show host popped into Matteo's Trattoria Saturday night in Boca Raton, FL -- where he and a group of pals were sitting near a makeshift stage ... where management had booked a singer for the night to croon to old-timey songs, like Sinatra and whatnot.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-8673c67c80b7b0685e3e6ba7e6f8db41-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-youtube-video-block canvas-youtube-video-block-blogroll canvas-youtube-video-block--default" id="cb-012b947e2b2dde7613f21f1857d32517">

         </div>
         <script id="cb-012b947e2b2dde7613f21f1857d32517-968146408-failed" type="text/x-consent-element">

         <script>
          wbq.push(function renderYoutubeVideoBlock() {
      var $target = $('#cb-012b947e2b2dde7613f21f1857d32517-968146408-target');
      var targetWidth = $target.width();

      function initPlayer(onReady) {
          new YT.Player('cb-012b947e2b2dde7613f21f1857d32517-968146408-target', {
            height: targetWidth / (16 / 9),
            host: 'https://www.youtube-nocookie.com',
            width: targetWidth,
            events: {
              'onReady': onReady,
            },
            playerVars: {
              'enablejsapi': 1,
              'origin': window.location.origin,
            },
          });
      }

      function cueVideo(e) {
        e.target.cueVideoById('6S4Nd0iH1l0', 0);
      }

      function insertSwipe(e) {
        var swipeDiv = document.createElement('div');
        swipeDiv.innerText = "Exclusive";
        swipeDiv.classList.add('media-swipe');
        swipeDiv.classList.add('youtube-video-block__media-swipe');
        e.target.getIframe().parentNode.prepend(swipeDiv);
      }

      function fail() {
        $target.html(document.getElementById('cb-012b947e2b2dde7613f21f1857d32517-968146408-failed').innerHTML);
      }

      function styleIframe(e) {
        var iframe = e.target.getIframe();
        iframe.classList.add('embed-responsive');
        if (!iframe.getAttribute('width')) {
          iframe.setAttribute('width', targetWidth);
        }
        if (!iframe.getAttribute('height')) {
          iframe.setAttribute('height', targetWidth / (16 / 9));
        }
      }

              window.TMZ.utils.loadYouTubeJs()
          .then(function initYouTubeBlock() {
            initPlayer(function onReady(e) {
              styleIframe(e);
              cueVideo(e);

        <!--/#cb-012b947e2b2dde7613f21f1857d32517-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-dc80e521de014c3448abf483928c5304">
         <p>
          We're told that toward the end of the guy's set and as it was nearing closing time, Jerry got up and spoke with the singer ... and then got on the mic himself to belt out EP's 'Love Me Tender.' As he sang, the crowd hooted and hollered ... clearly impressed with his pipes.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-dc80e521de014c3448abf483928c5304-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-495bd5eb34bd9d95cd1cc3f51a1e8b8a">
         <p>
          While the crowd might've been surprised over Jerry's smooth, silky voice ... it's actually nothing new. The guy stays singing 'LMT' ... or at least he was for years in honor of Elvis' birthday, Jan. 8. He did it back to back
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/2016/01/08/jerry-springer-elvis-impression-video/">
           <strong>
            in 2016
           </strong>
          </a>
          and
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/2017/01/06/jerry-springer-sings-elvis-presley-karaoke/">
           <strong>
            2017
           </strong>
          </a>
          at the same joint in Dallas.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-495bd5eb34bd9d95cd1cc3f51a1e8b8a-->

          wbq.push(function renderVideoBlock() {
        var page = window.TMZ.select(window.TMZ.selectors.getPage);
        // there is a weird bug with iPhone 6+ on iOS 9.3.4 where the spinner gets revealed even after its
        // event listener has been removed, so for now this stupid flag can correct for that.
        var isResolved = false;
        if (!page.isTurbolinksPreview) {
          function displayPlayer(player) {
            if (player.id === 'jwplayer-video-player-2c56d8ea-0763-58a0-a1d3-5e101f764458-1834379463-player') {
              player.getContainer().closest('.embed-responsive-item--jwplayer').classList.remove('invisible');
              return;
            }
            // a fallback video
            player.closest('.embed-responsive-item--jwplayer').classList.remove('invisible');
          }
          function fadeImageHolderAndFooter() {
            var imageHolder = document.getElementById('video-player-2c56d8ea-0763-58a0-a1d3-5e101f764458-1834379463-image-holder');
            var footer = document.getElementById('video-player-2c56d8ea-0763-58a0-a1d3-5e101f764458-1834379463-footer');
            if (imageHolder) {
              imageHolder.addEventListener('transitionend', removeImageHolder, { once: true });
              imageHolder.classList.add('video-block__image-holder-fade');
            }

            if (footer && !footer.classList.contains('hidden')) {
              footer.addEventListener('transitionend', removeFooter, { once: true });
              footer.classList.add('video-block__media-footer-fade');
            }
          }
          function removeImageHolder() {
            var imageHolder = document.getElementById('video-player-2c56d8ea-0763-58a0-a1d3-5e101f764458-1834379463-image-holder');
            if (imageHolder) {
              imageHolder.remove();
            }
          }
          function removeFooter() {
            var footer = document.getElementById('video-player-2c56d8ea-0763-58a0-a1d3-5e101f764458-1834379463-footer');
            if (footer) {
              footer.classList.add('hidden');
            }
          }
          function hideSpinner() {
            var spinner = document.getElementById('video-player-2c56d8ea-0763-58a0-a1d3-5e101f764458-1834379463-progress-spinner');
            spinner.classList.add('below');
            spinner.classList.remove('above');
          }
          function revealSpinner() {
            if (isResolved) {
              return;
            }
            var spinner = document.getElementById('video-player-2c56d8ea-0763-58a0-a1d3-5e101f764458-1834379463-progress-spinner');
            spinner.classList.add('above');
            spinner.classList.remove('below');
          }
          window.TMZ.videos.observe(document.getElementById('jwplayer-video-player-2c56d8ea-0763-58a0-a1d3-5e101f764458-1834379463'), {
                        onObserve: function() {
              document.getElementById('video-player-2c56d8ea-0763-58a0-a1d3-5e101f764458-1834379463-play-btn').addEventListener('mousemove', revealSpinner, { once: true });

              var playButton = document.getElementById('video-player-2c56d8ea-0763-58a0-a1d3-5e101f764458-1834379463-play-btn');

                    action: 'click'
                  }
                ));
              }, { once: true });
              hideSpinner();
            }
                      });
        }
      });

          wbq.push(function renderYoutubeVideoBlock() {
      var $target = $('#cb-094b94a945616c9f79624f1e0d45239b-144296962-target');
      var targetWidth = $target.width();

      function initPlayer(onReady) {
          new YT.Player('cb-094b94a945616c9f79624f1e0d45239b-144296962-target', {
            height: targetWidth / (16 / 9),
            host: 'https://www.youtube-nocookie.com',
            width: targetWidth,
            events: {
              'onReady': onReady,
            },
            playerVars: {
              'enablejsapi': 1,
              'origin': window.location.origin,
            },
          });
      }

      function cueVideo(e) {
        e.target.cueVideoById('OAvy-rvnQm4', 0);
      }

      function insertSwipe(e) {
        var swipeDiv = document.createElement('div');
        swipeDiv.innerText = null;
        swipeDiv.classList.add('media-swipe');
        swipeDiv.classList.add('youtube-video-block__media-swipe');
        e.target.getIframe().parentNode.prepend(swipeDiv);
      }

      function fail() {
        $target.html(document.getElementById('cb-094b94a945616c9f79624f1e0d45239b-144296962-failed').innerHTML);
      }

      function styleIframe(e) {
        var iframe = e.target.getIframe();
        iframe.classList.add('embed-responsive');
        if (!iframe.getAttribute('width')) {
          iframe.setAttribute('width', targetWidth);
        }
        if (!iframe.getAttribute('height')) {
          iframe.setAttribute('height', targetWidth / (16 / 9));
        }
      }

              window.TMZ.utils.loadYouTubeJs()
          .then(function initYouTubeBlock() {

              styleIframe(e);
              cueVideo(e);
                                        });
          }).catch(fail);
          });

        <!--/#cb-094b94a945616c9f79624f1e0d45239b-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-1c7cd9156a55196a2153949edbd0085b">
         <p>
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/people/wayne-gretzky/">
           <strong>
            Wayne Gretzky
           </strong>
          </a>
          was fighting back tears at his father's funeral this weekend -- especially during an emotional eulogy ... where he remembered the man as the ultimate hockey dad.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-1c7cd9156a55196a2153949edbd0085b-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-5e8cc8bd929eaae5a28e7cd050dcdbd7">
         <p>
          The NHL legend delivered remarks Saturday at the St. Mark's Anglican Church in Brantford, Ontario shortly after laying
          <strong>
           Walter Gretzky
          </strong>
          to rest. Wayne stepped up to the podium in front of a socially distanced crowd in the pews ... and reminisced about Walter's life. The service was limited to family.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-5e8cc8bd929eaae5a28e7cd050dcdbd7-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-image-block canvas-image-block-blogroll canvas-image-block--default" id="cb-6e51ea5dc1129ff9a00b69161000a95a">
         <div class="image-block">
          <img alt="" class="img-fluid image-block__img-fluid img-aspect-auto" loading="lazy" src="https://imagez.tmz.com/image/dc/4by3/2021/03/07/dc58b6a61ac444ef95c6f13bce88f9d3_md.jpg"/>
          <div class="image-block__card-footer">
           <span class="media-credit image-block__media-credit">
            AP
           </span>
          </div>
         </div>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-6e51ea5dc1129ff9a00b69161000a95a-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-7e4e2fef97b1d53a31558d0da1b63c5b">
         <p>
          He recounted a couple different stories that were pretty heartwarming -- one where Wayne says Walter insisted on going to a hockey tournament when he was young, this despite the fact his wife and Wayne's mom,
          <strong>
           Phyllis
          </strong>
          , was due to give birth at any moment.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-7e4e2fef97b1d53a31558d0da1b63c5b-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-bf6117227c370069fbcf567c1f1ab0b1">
         <p>
          Sure enough, she popped while he was away with Wayne ... and as people gave Walter a hard time about missing the birth of his own child, he hoisted up the first-place prize that Wayne and co. had won, and proudly said ... "Yes, but we got the trophy."
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-bf6117227c370069fbcf567c1f1ab0b1-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-image-block canvas-image-block-blogroll canvas-image-block--default" id="cb-9dd91a4044109efdf71b6a095135da05">
         <div class="image-block">
          <img alt="" class="img-fluid image-block__img-fluid img-aspect-auto" loading="lazy" src="https://imagez.tmz.com/image/8d/4by3/2021/03/05/8dfd9f3b0d824fa39c5706e11fc0d7a6_md.jpg"/>
          <div class="image-block__card-footer">
           <span class="media-credit image-block__media-credit">
            Getty
           </span>
          </div>
         </div>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-9dd91a4044109efdf71b6a095135da05-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-808d5946a1c0329ba33360df71e9381b">
         <p>
          Wayne went on to remember Walter as an incredibly proud Canadian and hockey's #1 fan. He said he loved his kids and grandkids ... and was always looking to give back to Wayne's fans as he grew in his career.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-808d5946a1c0329ba33360df71e9381b-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-cde26fd01d311b03c0777d2cd7e2a8d7">
         <p>
          WG said Walter was not afflicted with COVID, and
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/2021/03/05/wayne-gretzky-father-walter-dead/">
           <strong>
            his death
           </strong>
          </a>
          had nothing to do with the virus. He reiterated his dad suffered a bad hip injury as a result of his Parkinson's ... and was already in declining health. He thanked the crowd and those afar for sending food and well-wishes as the family stayed with him for 21 straight days in the hospital until he eventually passed Thursday.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-cde26fd01d311b03c0777d2cd7e2a8d7-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-image-block canvas-image-block-blogroll canvas-image-block--default" id="cb-fff1e9c1756c8e5562b968f9ceba1e41">
         <div class="image-block">
          <img alt="" class="img-fluid image-block__img-fluid img-aspect-auto" loading="lazy" src="https://imagez.tmz.com/image/70/4by3/2021/03/05/70c900b3534b43b6992f237a94f529d4_md.jpg"/>
          <div class="image-block__card-footer">
           <span class="media-credit image-block__media-credit">
            Getty
           </span>
          </div>
         </div>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-fff1e9c1756c8e5562b968f9ceba1e41-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-ac94211aad9fb446e48a30932b851a5c">
         <p>
          Toward the end of his speech, Wayne choked up and walked off stage ... and the audience gave him a slight round of applause.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-ac94211aad9fb446e48a30932b851a5c-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-dee46c149ecb1ca14d5a76fb45267fed">
         <p>
          Walter was 82.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-dee46c149ecb1ca14d5a76fb45267fed-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default canvas-block-is-last" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-5952bcce218791c4e1a1c3dc2322aaa4">
         <p>
          RIP
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-5952bcce218791c4e1a1c3dc2322aaa4-->

        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-c0ec76d1a02a6c197bd93fa2200ea59a">
         <p>
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/people/rush-limbaugh/">
           <strong>
            Rush Limbaugh
           </strong>
          </a>
          is the G.O.A.T. when it comes to radio hosts, and if you don't believe that ... just read his death certificate.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-c0ec76d1a02a6c197bd93fa2200ea59a-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-4ef5ef6717e68499872a61a4ee0df101">
         <p>
          According to
          <a href="https://dam.tmz.com/document/df/o/2021/03/04/dfed8f4960684a1dae64c8b09cd2f741.pdf" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
           <strong>
            the document
           </strong>
          </a>
          , obtained by TMZ, the conservative firebrand host's occupation is right there in black and white -- "GREATEST RADIO HOST OF ALL TIME." That's some pretty high praise.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-4ef5ef6717e68499872a61a4ee0df101-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-ad67d3d3786c4fd19b80440dd5727f21">
         <p>
          It's high praise for Rush that many, including his pal
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/people/donald-trump/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank" title="https://www.tmz.com/people/donald-trump/">
           <strong>
            Donald Trump
           </strong>
          </a>
          , would agree with -- but of course, there's probably those who'd strongly disagree.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-ad67d3d3786c4fd19b80440dd5727f21-->

            player.closest('.embed-responsive-item--jwplayer').classList.remove('invisible');
          }
          function fadeImageHolderAndFooter() {
            var imageHolder = document.getElementById('video-player-ca0626f9-6dfe-4725-b405-0f3bf20e7fac-1890717159-image-holder');
            var footer = document.getElementById('video-player-ca0626f9-6dfe-4725-b405-0f3bf20e7fac-1890717159-footer');
            if (imageHolder) {
              imageHolder.addEventListener('transitionend', removeImageHolder, { once: true });
              imageHolder.classList.add('video-block__image-holder-fade');
            }

            if (footer && !footer.classList.contains('hidden')) {
              footer.addEventListener('transitionend', removeFooter, { once: true });
              footer.classList.add('video-block__media-footer-fade');
            }
          }
          function removeImageHolder() {
            var imageHolder = document.getElementById('video-player-ca0626f9-6dfe-4725-b405-0f3bf20e7fac-1890717159-image-holder');
            if (imageHolder) {
              imageHolder.remove();
            }
          }
          function removeFooter() {
            var footer = document.getElementById('video-player-ca0626f9-6dfe-4725-b405-0f3bf20e7fac-1890717159-footer');
            if (footer) {
              footer.classList.add('hidden');
            }
          }
          function hideSpinner() {
            var spinner = document.getElementById('video-player-ca0626f9-6dfe-4725-b405-0f3bf20e7fac-1890717159-progress-spinner');
            spinner.classList.add('below');
            spinner.classList.remove('above');
          }
          function revealSpinner() {
            if (isResolved) {
              return;
            }
            var spinner = document.getElementById('video-player-ca0626f9-6dfe-4725-b405-0f3bf20e7fac-1890717159-progress-spinner');
            spinner.classList.add('above');
            spinner.classList.remove('below');
          }
          window.TMZ.videos.observe(document.getElementById('jwplayer-video-player-ca0626f9-6dfe-4725-b405-0f3bf20e7fac-1890717159'), {
                        onObserve: function() {
              document.getElementById('video-player-ca0626f9-6dfe-4725-b405-0f3bf20e7fac-1890717159-play-btn').addEventListener('mousemove', revealSpinner, { once: true });
            },
            onResolve: function(player) {
              isResolved = true;
              var playButton = document.getElementById('video-player-ca0626f9-6dfe-4725-b405-0f3bf20e7fac-1890717159-play-btn');
              playButton.removeEventListener('mousemove', revealSpinner);
              playButton.addEventListener('click', function() {
                displayPlayer(player);
                player.play();
                removeImageHolder();
                removeFooter();
                window.TMZ.dispatch(window.TMZ.actions.clickLink(
                  'https://www.tmz.com/videos/2021-02-17-021721-rush-limbaugh-1042877/',
                  null,
                  'tmz:video:ca0626f9-6dfe-4725-b405-0f3bf20e7fac',
                  null,
                  {
                    section: 'blogroll',
                    name: 'video',
                    action: 'click'
                  }
                ));
              }, { once: true });
              hideSpinner();
            }
                      });
        }
      });
         </script>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-561251049226c540e2b4b78965cf23fa-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-19c8ced124b72359088c6017a94c4e6c">
         <p>
          Remember, Trump
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/2020/02/05/rush-limbaugh-state-of-disbelief-presidential-medal-of-freedom/">
           <strong>
            presented Rush
           </strong>
          </a>
          with the Presidential Medal of Freedom for his achievements in radio -- but Florida Governor
          <strong>
           Ron DeSantis
          </strong>
          got
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/2021/02/23/fl-ag-commish-nikki-fried-wont-lower-flags-honor-rush-limbaugh-defies-gov-desantis/">
           <strong>
            some pushback
           </strong>
          </a>
          when he ordered flags lowered to honor Limbaugh after
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/2021/02/17/rush-limbaugh-dead-at-70-lung-cancer/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank" title="https://www.tmz.com/2021/02/17/rush-limbaugh-dead-at-70-lung-cancer/">
           <strong>
            his death last month
           </strong>
          </a>
          of lung cancer.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-19c8ced124b72359088c6017a94c4e6c-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-c49ff3feae80cb048853f278390ad1f5">
         <p>
          We know what you're thinking -- Rush probably had a big fan in the Palm Beach County Medical Examiner's Office who put that title on the death certificate.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-c49ff3feae80cb048853f278390ad1f5-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-62617eeaa70d0900c9cc6ddcf4e73cc7">
         <p>
          However, his wife,
          <strong>
           Kathryn Limbaugh
          </strong>
          , is listed as the person providing the info for the document, so it's most likely her handiwork.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-62617eeaa70d0900c9cc6ddcf4e73cc7-->

        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-7d8f309f19a4f497eae138a81fd52e6f">
         <p>
          "The Rush Limbaugh Show" was nationally syndicated, starting in 1988, and made him one of the premier voices in the conservative ranks, as well as one of the most listened to radio personalities.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-7d8f309f19a4f497eae138a81fd52e6f-->

       <div class="article__blocks">
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-image-block canvas-image-block-blogroll canvas-image-block--default canvas-block-is-first" id="cb-0e50f6608b9a5cb51a24e22345cd7ea4">
         <div class="image-block">
          <img alt="" class="img-fluid image-block__img-fluid img-aspect-auto" loading="lazy" src="https://imagez.tmz.com/image/a5/4by3/2021/03/07/a5dceb674ea7469693cab5a6f21aab45_md.jpg"/>
         </div>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-0e50f6608b9a5cb51a24e22345cd7ea4-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-aec145216aeee11c73c9cba2d95e0b1b">
         <p>
          The sound mixer from the award-winning movie, "Nomadland," has died after taking his own life ... and his father thinks the coronavirus pandemic may have played a part.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-aec145216aeee11c73c9cba2d95e0b1b-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-e7ee01fc22b2a3f4afa3280253092958">
         <p>
          <strong>
           Michael Wolf Snyder
          </strong>
          had not been heard from for several days, when his dad, psychiatrist Dr.
          <strong>
           David Snyder
          </strong>
          , went to check on him in his Queens apartment. David discovered his son's body.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-e7ee01fc22b2a3f4afa3280253092958-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-6191b49dffd499da6b6b8c211847ea2c">
         <p>
          Dr. Snyder says his son had battled severe depression for years.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-6191b49dffd499da6b6b8c211847ea2c-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-youtube-video-block canvas-youtube-video-block-blogroll canvas-youtube-video-block--default" id="cb-668f531d90ddd448c19904ca531e96aa">

      function styleIframe(e) {
        var iframe = e.target.getIframe();
        iframe.classList.add('embed-responsive');
        if (!iframe.getAttribute('width')) {
          iframe.setAttribute('width', targetWidth);
        }
        if (!iframe.getAttribute('height')) {
          iframe.setAttribute('height', targetWidth / (16 / 9));
        }
      }

              window.TMZ.utils.loadYouTubeJs()
          .then(function initYouTubeBlock() {
            initPlayer(function onReady(e) {
              styleIframe(e);
              cueVideo(e);
                                        });
          }).catch(fail);
          });
         </script>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-668f531d90ddd448c19904ca531e96aa-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-41bc18308c5f8f1f85395ca96ead33a9">
         <p>
          35-year-old Michael, who went by his middle name, Wolf, had achieved a lot professionally. In addition to the Golden-Globe winning "Nomadland," he worked on the Emmy-nominated show, "Good Omens." He also worked on the 2017 sci-fi flick, "Imitation Girl," and the 2018 movie, "The Amaranth."
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-41bc18308c5f8f1f85395ca96ead33a9-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-9d6be3189e841bd6eace7d4d1e04b5c0">
         <p>
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/people/frances-mcdormand/">
           <strong>
            Frances McDormand
           </strong>
          </a>
          , the star of "Nomadland," said, "Wolf recorded our heartbeats. Our every breath. For me, he is 'Nomadland.'"
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-9d6be3189e841bd6eace7d4d1e04b5c0-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-e7ed136499ef9515c12794a5f576a1a4">
         <p>
          Wolf worked as a boom operator and sound mixer with filmmaker
          <strong>
           Chloe Zhao
          </strong>
          for "The Rider," and Zhao said, "I always looked at Wolf after each take. I didn't wear headphones on the set so I heavily relied on Wolf to be my ears. He would nod at me with a happy grin, or tears in his eyes, or sometimes he would discreetly signal, 'one more.'"
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-e7ed136499ef9515c12794a5f576a1a4-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-bad61d9ed5e9222abb8a6eba1187a9ba">
         <p>
          Wolf's dad said he didn't know how deeply his son had been struggling with depression, saying, "I am a psychiatrist who was not able to save his own son, partly because he would not share the depth of his pain," adding, "For most people, this is an illness that waxes and wanes over the years. I'm sure it was difficult for Michael that he spent most of the last year alone in his small, Queens apartment, being responsible about dealing with the coronavirus." He went on ... "In spite of this, we all believed he was doing well, and for most of this past year I think he was."
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-bad61d9ed5e9222abb8a6eba1187a9ba-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default canvas-block-is-last" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-d42c7ee4f405fce2189dc494a12bafc2">
         <p>
          Wolf was 35. RIP
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-d42c7ee4f405fce2189dc494a12bafc2-->
       </div>

        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-af5f47102666450bfc0764fdbc9a618a">
         <p>
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/people/meghan-markle/">
           <strong>
            Meghan Markle
           </strong>
          </a>
          is taking off the gloves in her highly-anticipated/feared interview with
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/people/oprah-winfrey/">
           <strong>
            Oprah
           </strong>
          </a>
          , but she reportedly is nothing but nice to a Royal with whom she had issues ...
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/people/kate-middleton/">
           <strong>
            Kate Middleton
           </strong>
          </a>
          .
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-af5f47102666450bfc0764fdbc9a618a-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-01a983eea9aa7b91e2759731a57f338e">
         <p>
          Markle has only kind words for her sister-in-law, according to NY Post sources.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-01a983eea9aa7b91e2759731a57f338e-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-image-block canvas-image-block-blogroll canvas-image-block--default" id="cb-8aee1f5c5613c54b9cb9ae6edaa44121">
         <div class="image-block">
          <img alt="" class="img-fluid image-block__img-fluid img-aspect-auto" loading="lazy" src="https://imagez.tmz.com/image/dd/4by3/2021/03/07/dd6986c5e6d34ef5a3bba195a6e3b648_md.jpg"/>
          <div class="image-block__card-footer">
           <span class="media-credit image-block__media-credit">
            Getty
           </span>
          </div>
         </div>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-8aee1f5c5613c54b9cb9ae6edaa44121-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-0438af005bb262610e7686c70ca7ff40">
         <p>
          The Palace reportedly is overwrought with worry over Sunday's sit-down, and an obvious concern is the now widely-reported rift between Meghan and Kate. There have been numerous stories about Kate being reduced to tears over Meghan's alleged demands revolving around Meghan's wedding.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-0438af005bb262610e7686c70ca7ff40-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-c1ec84eb2781a86f6dff797275b9a5f2">

          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/people/prince-william/">
           <strong>
            William
           </strong>
          </a>
          . William and
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/people/prince-harry/">
           <strong>
            Harry
           </strong>
          </a>
          have had a fractured relationship for a while now ... when
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/2020/01/08/prince-harry-meghan-markle-step-down-senior-royals/">
           <strong>
            Harry left
           </strong>
          </a>
          England we're told the 2 were barely speaking.
         </p>
        </section>

            if (player.id === 'jwplayer-video-player-339513f3-5ebb-4906-8c10-46a56a9f5086-1397301879-player') {

            }

          }
          function fadeImageHolderAndFooter() {
            var imageHolder = document.getElementById('video-player-339513f3-5ebb-4906-8c10-46a56a9f5086-1397301879-image-holder');
            var footer = document.getElementById('video-player-339513f3-5ebb-4906-8c10-46a56a9f5086-1397301879-footer');
            if (imageHolder) {
              imageHolder.addEventListener('transitionend', removeImageHolder, { once: true });
              imageHolder.classList.add('video-block__image-holder-fade');
            }

            if (footer && !footer.classList.contains('hidden')) {
              footer.addEventListener('transitionend', removeFooter, { once: true });
              footer.classList.add('video-block__media-footer-fade');
            }
          }
          function removeImageHolder() {
            var imageHolder = document.getElementById('video-player-339513f3-5ebb-4906-8c10-46a56a9f5086-1397301879-image-holder');
            if (imageHolder) {

          function removeFooter() {
            var footer = document.getElementById('video-player-339513f3-5ebb-4906-8c10-46a56a9f5086-1397301879-footer');
            if (footer) {
              footer.classList.add('hidden');
            }
          }
          function hideSpinner() {
            var spinner = document.getElementById('video-player-339513f3-5ebb-4906-8c10-46a56a9f5086-1397301879-progress-spinner');
            spinner.classList.add('below');
            spinner.classList.remove('above');
          }
          function revealSpinner() {
            if (isResolved) {
              return;
            }
            var spinner = document.getElementById('video-player-339513f3-5ebb-4906-8c10-46a56a9f5086-1397301879-progress-spinner');
            spinner.classList.add('above');
            spinner.classList.remove('below');
          }
          window.TMZ.videos.observe(document.getElementById('jwplayer-video-player-339513f3-5ebb-4906-8c10-46a56a9f5086-1397301879'), {
                        onObserve: function() {
              document.getElementById('video-player-339513f3-5ebb-4906-8c10-46a56a9f5086-1397301879-play-btn').addEventListener('mousemove', revealSpinner, { once: true });
            },
            onResolve: function(player) {
              isResolved = true;
              var playButton = document.getElementById('video-player-339513f3-5ebb-4906-8c10-46a56a9f5086-1397301879-play-btn');
              playButton.removeEventListener('mousemove', revealSpinner);
              playButton.addEventListener('click', function() {
                displayPlayer(player);
                player.play();
                removeImageHolder();
                removeFooter();
                window.TMZ.dispatch(window.TMZ.actions.clickLink(
                  'https://www.tmz.com/videos/2021-03-05-030521-oprah-meghan-markle-1050777/',
                  null,
                  'tmz:video:339513f3-5ebb-4906-8c10-46a56a9f5086',
                  null,
                  {
                    section: 'blogroll',
                    name: 'video',
                    action: 'click'
                  }
                ));
              }, { once: true });
              hideSpinner();
            }
                      });
        }
      });
         </script>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-2b8f96c57b98b21ec10b535ff84fc361-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-fdd53022b6037f8d43e834c25bcef2fd">
         <p>
          The interview, however, justifies cause for concern among the Royal Fam. Meghan goes after The Firm hard, saying
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/2021/03/05/meghan-markle-accuses-buckingham-palace-queen-controlling-oprah-interview/">
           <strong>
            she was silenced
           </strong>
          </a>
          , lorded over and smeared.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-fdd53022b6037f8d43e834c25bcef2fd-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default canvas-block-is-last" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-5a30d4f1471372ca852b103af303c6ef">
         <p>
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/people/queen-elizabeth-ii/">
           <strong>
            Queen Elizabeth
           </strong>
          </a>
          will go before the cameras in England hours before Meghan's interview airs, asking her country for unity. It may be a futile effort, because the buzz is the Oprah interview amounts to a declaration of war.
         </p>
        </section>

        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-a6ebb95487a8361dc54b874bc94c4935">
         <p>
          UFC fighter
          <strong>
           Tim Elliott
          </strong>
          was multi-tasking Saturday night as he pounded away at his opponent, accusing him of beating his ex-girlfriend ... something the opponent's manager calls "reckless slander."
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-a6ebb95487a8361dc54b874bc94c4935-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-twitter-tweet-block canvas-twitter-tweet-block-blogroll canvas-twitter-tweet-block--default" id="cb-2f56d931cf3bb95dd6ba4cd602b04ae8">

        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-3bbb99ff78d2b85d7bbf084fd1bb3add">
         <p>
          Elliott was dominating the flyweight fight to an empty arena, when Elliott appeared to say, "I heard you choked your girl in 2018. Are you a woman beater? She messaged me." The opponent,
          <strong>
           Jordan Espinosa
          </strong>
          , responded, "Did she? You don't know the whole story." Elliott shot back, "I know enough," to which Espinosa said, "You don't know s***."
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-3bbb99ff78d2b85d7bbf084fd1bb3add-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-dd12105b18d8f4c7ac3e568d17f7cff1">
         <p>
          Elliott won the fight by unanimous decision. When it was over, Espinosa's manager,
          <strong>
           Bryan Hamper,
          </strong>
          called the accusation, "Reckless slander."
         </p>
        </section>

        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default canvas-block-is-last" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-d48bf12e7579492d33bc528bd935c73b">
         <p>
          After the fight, Elliott told reporters, "I didn't say that for anybody else to hear, because I don't know the whole story." He says he was messaged texts and photos between Espinosa and a woman and there were photos of the woman with choke marks around her neck. He added, "... it's not something I wanted the whole world to hear. That was supposed to be between him and I. I didn't know the mic was going to pick up on it."
         </p>

         <h2 class="article__header-title">

          </span>

        </a>

         <ul class="social social--sm">
