        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-image-block canvas-image-block-blogroll canvas-image-block--default canvas-block-is-first" id="cb-084100526a6336faac2a189b20bcea0a">
         <div class="image-block">
          <img alt="" class="img-fluid image-block__img-fluid img-aspect-auto" loading="lazy" src="https://imagez.tmz.com/image/c1/4by3/2021/03/07/c1d281629fbe442dac24f656430fa705_md.jpg"/>
         </div>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-084100526a6336faac2a189b20bcea0a-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-c0d3922343cf53e5d1da9bbb81ee4155">
         <p>
          This is a Ted Lasso-type feel-good moment, as 2 cops saved a dog that fell in icy waters.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-c0d3922343cf53e5d1da9bbb81ee4155-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-f1f223f52ff0708b92abb8f93b0aba2a">
         <p>
          The rescue went down Thursday in the village of Manteno, Illinois, when the PD got a call, "There's a big dog in the water about four houses down."
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-f1f223f52ff0708b92abb8f93b0aba2a-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-youtube-video-block canvas-youtube-video-block-blogroll canvas-youtube-video-block--default" id="cb-4e5a7e20c9aeeb84ce0b759c074ceffb">

         </div>

         </script>

              'onReady': onReady,
            },

      }

      }

        iframe.classList.add('embed-responsive');
        if (!iframe.getAttribute('width')) {
          iframe.setAttribute('width', targetWidth);

        <!--/#cb-4e5a7e20c9aeeb84ce0b759c074ceffb-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-27223d4a485f2892008af4137e409535">
         <p>
          That canine's a lucky dog, thanks to officers
          <strong>
           Quincey Spears
          </strong>
          and
          <strong>
           Jessica Rourke
          </strong>
          , who answered the call and sprung into action. They got a paddleboat to get near the struggling K-9, using a pole to help reach the dog, to no avail.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-27223d4a485f2892008af4137e409535-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-0806c9444877a2130da2029af2fecb19">
         <p>
          So, their only remaining option was to jump in the frigid water, along with a few good Samaritans, to save the pooch.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-0806c9444877a2130da2029af2fecb19-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-40cac98fc6d70e729da90afe32e03d5f">
         <p>
          Officer Spears explained what happened ... "When he was walking on the ice, he went into a spot where the sun was beating down on the ice, and it actually potentially melted that part of the ice, which the dog fell in."
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-40cac98fc6d70e729da90afe32e03d5f-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default canvas-block-is-last" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-3e743cea75b270b7dd0a94450c48accd">
         <p>
          The dog is safe and sound, and the 2 cops ... they're ok as well, and might we add, a little heroic to boot!
         </p>
        </section>

         <script>
          wbq.push(function renderVideoBlock() {
        var page = window.TMZ.select(window.TMZ.selectors.getPage);
        // there is a weird bug with iPhone 6+ on iOS 9.3.4 where the spinner gets revealed even after its
        // event listener has been removed, so for now this stupid flag can correct for that.
        var isResolved = false;
        if (!page.isTurbolinksPreview) {
          function displayPlayer(player) {
            if (player.id === 'jwplayer-video-player-cb75a0db-286f-491e-9f8c-5be75352617f-1672610607-player') {
              player.getContainer().closest('.embed-responsive-item--jwplayer').classList.remove('invisible');
              return;
            }
            // a fallback video
            player.closest('.embed-responsive-item--jwplayer').classList.remove('invisible');
          }
          function fadeImageHolderAndFooter() {
            var imageHolder = document.getElementById('video-player-cb75a0db-286f-491e-9f8c-5be75352617f-1672610607-image-holder');
            var footer = document.getElementById('video-player-cb75a0db-286f-491e-9f8c-5be75352617f-1672610607-footer');
            if (imageHolder) {
              imageHolder.addEventListener('transitionend', removeImageHolder, { once: true });
              imageHolder.classList.add('video-block__image-holder-fade');
            }

            if (footer && !footer.classList.contains('hidden')) {
              footer.addEventListener('transitionend', removeFooter, { once: true });
              footer.classList.add('video-block__media-footer-fade');
            }
          }
          function removeImageHolder() {
            var imageHolder = document.getElementById('video-player-cb75a0db-286f-491e-9f8c-5be75352617f-1672610607-image-holder');
            if (imageHolder) {
              imageHolder.remove();
            }
          }
          function removeFooter() {
            var footer = document.getElementById('video-player-cb75a0db-286f-491e-9f8c-5be75352617f-1672610607-footer');
            if (footer) {
              footer.classList.add('hidden');
            }
          }
          function hideSpinner() {
            var spinner = document.getElementById('video-player-cb75a0db-286f-491e-9f8c-5be75352617f-1672610607-progress-spinner');
            spinner.classList.add('below');
            spinner.classList.remove('above');
          }
          function revealSpinner() {
            if (isResolved) {
              return;
            }
            var spinner = document.getElementById('video-player-cb75a0db-286f-491e-9f8c-5be75352617f-1672610607-progress-spinner');
            spinner.classList.add('above');
            spinner.classList.remove('below');
          }
          window.TMZ.videos.observe(document.getElementById('jwplayer-video-player-cb75a0db-286f-491e-9f8c-5be75352617f-1672610607'), {
                        onObserve: function() {
              document.getElementById('video-player-cb75a0db-286f-491e-9f8c-5be75352617f-1672610607-play-btn').addEventListener('mousemove', revealSpinner, { once: true });
            },
            onResolve: function(player) {
              isResolved = true;
              var playButton = document.getElementById('video-player-cb75a0db-286f-491e-9f8c-5be75352617f-1672610607-play-btn');
              playButton.removeEventListener('mousemove', revealSpinner);
              playButton.addEventListener('click', function() {
                displayPlayer(player);
                player.play();
                removeImageHolder();
                removeFooter();
                window.TMZ.dispatch(window.TMZ.actions.clickLink(
                  'https://www.tmz.com/videos/2021-03-07-030721-joseph-perez-bodycam-1051445/',
                  null,
                  'tmz:video:cb75a0db-286f-491e-9f8c-5be75352617f',
                  null,
                  {
                    section: 'blogroll',
                    name: 'video',
                    action: 'click'
                  }
                ));
              }, { once: true });
              hideSpinner();
            }
                      });
        }
      });

        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-e24fd0e7830f9f87d1a5c72f3c6f7af4">
         <p>
          The Fresno Police Dept. was ordered to release body cam video that graphically shows yet another chokehold-related homicide ... and it's extremely hard to watch.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-e24fd0e7830f9f87d1a5c72f3c6f7af4-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-7982ae2e67dc8286bdf974202bdce9f3">
         <p>
          The incident occurred in 2017 ...
          <strong>
           Joseph Perez
          </strong>
          had suffered a mental breakdown and police were called to help. As cops tried restraining the 41-year-old, you hear him scream, "I can't breathe," and "Let me redeem myself."
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-7982ae2e67dc8286bdf974202bdce9f3-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-4b2acb502663d265fa84a90e61255c8d">
         <p>
          The officers tell him to calm down and breathe, but Perez is clearly fighting for air and it becomes a vicious cycle -- the longer his airway is restricted, the more agitated he becomes and the officers use his resistance to justify more compression.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-4b2acb502663d265fa84a90e61255c8d-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-image-block canvas-image-block-blogroll canvas-image-block--default" id="cb-9ebc00edc6b30c6a5b6b30e8fe87b2e5">
         <div class="image-block">
          <img alt="" class="img-fluid image-block__img-fluid img-aspect-auto" loading="lazy" src="https://imagez.tmz.com/image/68/4by3/2021/03/07/68a4a992828d49b4a2dca255efc76cda_md.jpg"/>
         </div>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-9ebc00edc6b30c6a5b6b30e8fe87b2e5-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-a02136a4f74805f213782683674f39e3">
         <p>
          Paramedics arrived and told a cop to sit on the backboard they brought to carry Perez into the ambulance. The backboard was placed on Perez's back as his head was face down on the ground.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-a02136a4f74805f213782683674f39e3-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-62df83443f3c00292fe9801a2e7b940a">
         <p>
          Perez died in an ambulance on the way to the hospital.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-62df83443f3c00292fe9801a2e7b940a-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-b5fa92934f9135195b3416b68c476621">
         <p>
          Perez's family has filed a wrongful death lawsuit against the officers, the City and County of Fresno and the ambulance company.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-b5fa92934f9135195b3416b68c476621-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-177483b84270145bcddbb3532033673e">
         <p>
          <strong>
           Neil Gehlawat
          </strong>
          , the lawyer for the Perez family, says, "Compression asphyxia during restraining is all too common, and we hope to expose this pervasive tactic used by law enforcement officers across the country."
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-177483b84270145bcddbb3532033673e-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default canvas-block-is-last" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-1fe29baf46a37bdf54b45e885aeef681">
         <p>
          The Sheriff's Dept. reportedly declined comment, citing the ongoing lawsuit.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-1fe29baf46a37bdf54b45e885aeef681-->

        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-image-block canvas-image-block-blogroll canvas-image-block--default canvas-block-is-first" id="cb-7fb0c3b079bd6f9e054959b44b44d63c">
         <div class="image-block">
          <img alt="" class="img-fluid image-block__img-fluid img-aspect-auto" loading="lazy" src="https://imagez.tmz.com/image/1f/4by3/2021/03/05/1ff57ee80194419595821ee0f18f810c_md.jpg"/>
          <div class="media-swipe image-block__media-swipe">
           Exclusive
          </div>
         </div>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-7fb0c3b079bd6f9e054959b44b44d63c-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-0030e1729d8939b64214ca58d6e30c84">
         <p>
          <strong>
           Tessica Brown
          </strong>
          tried getting out of another sticky situation by crowdfunding ... or at least that's what an imposter had people believing before GoFundMe dropped the hammer.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-0030e1729d8939b64214ca58d6e30c84-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-017d3b35d72347934edf33e95a6adc43">
         <p>
          So get this ... someone tried to capitalize on Tessica's Gorilla Glue fame and misfortune by posting a GoFundMe page pretending to be her. The imposter even posted what appears to be a $186k hospital bill.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-017d3b35d72347934edf33e95a6adc43-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-image-block canvas-image-block-blogroll canvas-image-block--default" id="cb-5f31bec4a58bf889399cc85e32a368b5">
         <div class="image-block">
          <img alt="" class="img-fluid image-block__img-fluid img-aspect-auto" loading="lazy" src="https://imagez.tmz.com/image/e2/4by3/2021/03/05/e2c6bab2ea1a4b418742e7226fd37363_md.jpg"/>
         </div>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-5f31bec4a58bf889399cc85e32a368b5-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-b28e573e3fe099d7f63c8c87ac48c51f">
         <p>
          As you can see, the imposter claimed the hospital was charging her for her medical bills after it found out she was raising money online. This person even roped in Tessica's real GoFundMe dilemma ... ya know, the alleged fraud claims that were
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/2021/02/18/tessica-brown-gorilla-glue-gofundme-money-investigation-charity/">
           <strong>
            later debunked
           </strong>
          </a>
          .
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-b28e573e3fe099d7f63c8c87ac48c51f-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-30fdb6b3e63f7859adcd3e4cfa390102">
         <p>
          The imposter's "bill" looked legit enough to dupe some peeps, 'cause the account raised around $500.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-30fdb6b3e63f7859adcd3e4cfa390102-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-0c44e38533bea0490c8fc06de7faa16c">
         <p>
          Don't worry, the imposter never got the dough because a rep for GoFundMe tells TMZ it suspended the account as soon as it got wind of it.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-0c44e38533bea0490c8fc06de7faa16c-->

         <script>
          wbq.push(function renderVideoBlock() {
        var page = window.TMZ.select(window.TMZ.selectors.getPage);
        // there is a weird bug with iPhone 6+ on iOS 9.3.4 where the spinner gets revealed even after its
        // event listener has been removed, so for now this stupid flag can correct for that.
        var isResolved = false;
        if (!page.isTurbolinksPreview) {
          function displayPlayer(player) {
            if (player.id === 'jwplayer-video-player-71958bac-68eb-45ba-a565-d91d59058401-714990426-player') {
              player.getContainer().closest('.embed-responsive-item--jwplayer').classList.remove('invisible');
              return;
            }
            // a fallback video
            player.closest('.embed-responsive-item--jwplayer').classList.remove('invisible');
          }
          function fadeImageHolderAndFooter() {
            var imageHolder = document.getElementById('video-player-71958bac-68eb-45ba-a565-d91d59058401-714990426-image-holder');
            var footer = document.getElementById('video-player-71958bac-68eb-45ba-a565-d91d59058401-714990426-footer');
            if (imageHolder) {
              imageHolder.addEventListener('transitionend', removeImageHolder, { once: true });
              imageHolder.classList.add('video-block__image-holder-fade');
            }

            if (footer && !footer.classList.contains('hidden')) {
              footer.addEventListener('transitionend', removeFooter, { once: true });
              footer.classList.add('video-block__media-footer-fade');
            }
          }
          function removeImageHolder() {
            var imageHolder = document.getElementById('video-player-71958bac-68eb-45ba-a565-d91d59058401-714990426-image-holder');
            if (imageHolder) {
              imageHolder.remove();
            }
          }
          function removeFooter() {
            var footer = document.getElementById('video-player-71958bac-68eb-45ba-a565-d91d59058401-714990426-footer');
            if (footer) {
              footer.classList.add('hidden');
            }
          }
          function hideSpinner() {
            var spinner = document.getElementById('video-player-71958bac-68eb-45ba-a565-d91d59058401-714990426-progress-spinner');
            spinner.classList.add('below');
            spinner.classList.remove('above');
          }
          function revealSpinner() {
            if (isResolved) {
              return;
            }
            var spinner = document.getElementById('video-player-71958bac-68eb-45ba-a565-d91d59058401-714990426-progress-spinner');
            spinner.classList.add('above');
            spinner.classList.remove('below');
          }
          window.TMZ.videos.observe(document.getElementById('jwplayer-video-player-71958bac-68eb-45ba-a565-d91d59058401-714990426'), {
                        onObserve: function() {
              document.getElementById('video-player-71958bac-68eb-45ba-a565-d91d59058401-714990426-play-btn').addEventListener('mousemove', revealSpinner, { once: true });
            },
            onResolve: function(player) {
              isResolved = true;
              var playButton = document.getElementById('video-player-71958bac-68eb-45ba-a565-d91d59058401-714990426-play-btn');
              playButton.removeEventListener('mousemove', revealSpinner);
              playButton.addEventListener('click', function() {
                displayPlayer(player);
                player.play();
                removeImageHolder();
                removeFooter();
                window.TMZ.dispatch(window.TMZ.actions.clickLink(
                  'https://www.tmz.com/videos/2021-02-05-020521-tessica-brown-4920870/',
                  null,
                  'tmz:video:71958bac-68eb-45ba-a565-d91d59058401',
                  null,
                  {
                    section: 'blogroll',
                    name: 'video',
                    action: 'click'
                  }
                ));
              }, { once: true });
              hideSpinner();
            }
                      });
        }
      });
         </script>

        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-25d20a047ef8c73c00e5cae425867f87">
         <p>
          The fake account was sketchy to begin with ... 'cause the imposter's goal was only $25k but the bill totaled nearly $200k.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-25d20a047ef8c73c00e5cae425867f87-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default canvas-block-is-last" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-46245fb8d00759e0d6650f587181ee78">
         <p>
          Tessica's manager,
          <strong>
           Gina Rodriguez
          </strong>
          , tells TMZ ... she's seen several fake Twitter and GoFundMe pages trying to piggyback off Tessica. She warns, if you see one, DO NOT donate because Tessica doesn't need money -- she's doing well now, thanks to deals and her daycare and dance biz ventures.
         </p>
        </section>

          wbq.push(function renderVideoBlock() {
        var page = window.TMZ.select(window.TMZ.selectors.getPage);
        // there is a weird bug with iPhone 6+ on iOS 9.3.4 where the spinner gets revealed even after its
        // event listener has been removed, so for now this stupid flag can correct for that.
        var isResolved = false;
        if (!page.isTurbolinksPreview) {
          function displayPlayer(player) {
            if (player.id === 'jwplayer-video-player-202575ed-2626-4f6c-9523-bcfab3a804eb-2048857763-player') {
              player.getContainer().closest('.embed-responsive-item--jwplayer').classList.remove('invisible');
              return;
            }
            // a fallback video
            player.closest('.embed-responsive-item--jwplayer').classList.remove('invisible');
          }
          function fadeImageHolderAndFooter() {
            var imageHolder = document.getElementById('video-player-202575ed-2626-4f6c-9523-bcfab3a804eb-2048857763-image-holder');
            var footer = document.getElementById('video-player-202575ed-2626-4f6c-9523-bcfab3a804eb-2048857763-footer');
            if (imageHolder) {
              imageHolder.addEventListener('transitionend', removeImageHolder, { once: true });
              imageHolder.classList.add('video-block__image-holder-fade');
            }

            if (footer && !footer.classList.contains('hidden')) {
              footer.addEventListener('transitionend', removeFooter, { once: true });
              footer.classList.add('video-block__media-footer-fade');
            }
          }
          function removeImageHolder() {
            var imageHolder = document.getElementById('video-player-202575ed-2626-4f6c-9523-bcfab3a804eb-2048857763-image-holder');
            if (imageHolder) {
              imageHolder.remove();
            }
          }
          function removeFooter() {
            var footer = document.getElementById('video-player-202575ed-2626-4f6c-9523-bcfab3a804eb-2048857763-footer');
            if (footer) {
              footer.classList.add('hidden');
            }
          }
          function hideSpinner() {
            var spinner = document.getElementById('video-player-202575ed-2626-4f6c-9523-bcfab3a804eb-2048857763-progress-spinner');
            spinner.classList.add('below');
            spinner.classList.remove('above');
          }
          function revealSpinner() {
            if (isResolved) {
              return;
            }
            var spinner = document.getElementById('video-player-202575ed-2626-4f6c-9523-bcfab3a804eb-2048857763-progress-spinner');
            spinner.classList.add('above');
            spinner.classList.remove('below');
          }
          window.TMZ.videos.observe(document.getElementById('jwplayer-video-player-202575ed-2626-4f6c-9523-bcfab3a804eb-2048857763'), {
                        onObserve: function() {
              document.getElementById('video-player-202575ed-2626-4f6c-9523-bcfab3a804eb-2048857763-play-btn').addEventListener('mousemove', revealSpinner, { once: true });
            },
            onResolve: function(player) {
              isResolved = true;
              var playButton = document.getElementById('video-player-202575ed-2626-4f6c-9523-bcfab3a804eb-2048857763-play-btn');
              playButton.removeEventListener('mousemove', revealSpinner);
              playButton.addEventListener('click', function() {
                displayPlayer(player);
                player.play();
                removeImageHolder();
                removeFooter();
                window.TMZ.dispatch(window.TMZ.actions.clickLink(
                  'https://www.tmz.com/videos/2021-03-03-030321-jeff-george-jr-1049793/',

                  null,
                  {
                    section: 'blogroll',
                    name: 'video',
                    action: 'click'
                  }
                ));
              }, { once: true });
              hideSpinner();
            }
                      });
        }

         <p>
          <strong>
           Jeff George Jr.
          </strong>
          says he's so hellbent on following in his famous dad's NFL footsteps ... he's straight-up willing to sacrifice his life for an opportunity to play in the league.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-667c0b6ff7afbdac98b8db2c069f2e8b-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-ee9447765dd9b1b417469d743b54c280">
         <p>
          The oldest son of the legendary quarterback broke it all down for
          <strong>
           TMZ Sports
          </strong>
          ... saying he's telling NFL scouts he's that committed to being The Shield's next great QB.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-ee9447765dd9b1b417469d743b54c280-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-7646f5c1a7484e1140daee217b50bc91">
         <p>
          "They're getting a guy that's willing to put his life on the line for this," 24-year-old George Jr. said of what NFL teams will get from him if they draft him. "I don't want to do anything else."
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-7646f5c1a7484e1140daee217b50bc91-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-23af0274de0489134ec6db4de7b43a77">
         <p>
          "I put my blood, sweat, tears into this game. I love it more than anything."
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-23af0274de0489134ec6db4de7b43a77-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-78313db62bce633bdddd3b6f659f43f7">
         <p>
          JG2 started his college football career at Illinois and then went to Michigan before landing at Pitt, where he only played in 2 games in the 2019 season. He's 6'3", 220 lbs and just like his dad, he's got a cannon for an arm.
         </p>
        </section>

         <p>
          COVID screwed up his plans to show out in 2020 -- but George Jr. is now trying to showcase his skills for NFL teams at
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/people/brandon-tyrone-marshall/">

          His message to teams is simple ... "You're gonna get a guy who's the hardest worker in the building, super competitive and ultimately has a drive to win."
         </p>

           Jeff George Sr.

Aaron","bio":"Baseball's all-time home run king, Hank Aaron did more than hit home runs. Sure, Aaron led the National League (NL) four times, he also was a two-time batting champion and led the league in RBIs four times and runs scored three times. He won the NL's Most Valuable Player award in 1957 and has a lifetime batting average of .305. Aaron got his start playing for the Indianapolis Clowns, of the Negro Leagues before signing on with the Milwaukee Braves. He played at their minor league team in Eau Claire, Wis., one of the first black players there, and was brought up by the Braves in 1954. For the next 23 years, Aaron clobbered Major League pitchers. Never a charismatic player, Aaron often let his bat do the talking. He was the subject of intense media scrutiny in 1973-74 when he approached Babe Ruth's hallowed home run record. Aaron received more than 10,000 letters (most of them hate mail and even death threats) during the off-season claiming he should not break the record. Ever the ultimate professional and gentleman, he ignored the insults and slurs and went about the opening season in 1974. On April 8, 1974, Aaron hit his 715th home run, breaking Ruth's record and in doing so, received the undying support of the fans. He finished with 755 overall before retiring after the 1976 season. Aaron was elected to baseball's Hall of Fame in 1982, and now works in the front office for the Atlanta He had a twin brother who was stillborn. In September 1948, Elvis and his parents moved to Memphis, Tennessee where he attended Humes High School. In 1953, he attended the senior prom with the current girl he was courting, Regis Wilson. After graduating from high school in Memphis, Elvis took odd jobs working as a movie theater usher and a truck driver for Crown Electric Company. He began singing locally as \"The Hillbilly Cat\", then signed with a local recording company, and then with RCA in 1955.\n\nElvis did much to establish early rock and roll music. He began his career as a performer of rockabilly, an up-tempo fusion of country music and rhythm and blues, with a strong backbeat. His novel versions of existing songs, mixing 'black' and 'white' sounds, made him popular - and controversial - as did his uninhibited stage and television performances. He recorded songs in the rock and roll genre, with tracks like \"Jailhouse Rock\" and \"Hound Dog\" later embodying the style. Presley had a versatile voice and had unusually wide success encompassing other genres, including gospel, blues, ballads and pop music. Teenage girls became hysterical over his blatantly sexual gyrations, particularly the one that got him nicknamed \"Elvis the Pelvis\" (television cameras were not permitted to film below his waist).\n\nIn 1956, following his six television appearances on The Dorsey Brothers' \"Stage Show\", Elvis was cast in his first acting role, in a supporting part in Love Me Tender (1956), the first of 33 movies he starred in.\n\nIn 1958, Elvis was drafted into the military, and relocated to Bad Nauheim, Germany. There he met and fell in love with 14-year old army damsel Priscilla Ann Wagner (Priscilla Presley), whom he would eventually marry after an eight-year courtship, and with whom he had his only child, Lisa Marie Presley. Elvis' military service and the \"British Invasion\" of the 1960s reduced his concerts, though not his movie\/recording income.\n\nThrough the 1960s, Elvis settled in Hollywood, where he starred in the majority of his thirty-three movies, mainly musicals, acting alongside some of the most well known actors in Hollywood. Critics panned most of his films, but they did very well at the box office, earning upwards of $150 million total. His last fiction film, Change of Habit (1969), deals with several social issues; romance within the clergy, an autistic child, almost unheard of in 1969, rape, and mob violence. It has recently received critical acclaim.\n\nElvis made a comeback in the 1970s with live concert appearances starting in early 1970 in Las Vegas with over 57 sold-out shows. He toured throughout the United States, appearing on-stage in over 500 live appearances, many of them sold out shows. His marriage ended in divorce, and the stress of constantly traveling as well as his increasing weight gain and dependence upon stimulants and depressants took their toll.\n\nElvis Presley died at age 42 on August 16, 1977 at his mansion in Graceland, near Memphis, shocking his fans worldwide. At the time of his death, he had sold more than 600 million singles and albums. Since his death, Graceland has become a shrine for millions of followers worldwide. Elvis impersonators and purported sightings have become stock subjects for humorists. To date, Elvis Presley is the only performer to have been inducted into three separate music 'Halls of Fame'. Throughout his career, he set records for concert attendance, television ratings and recordings sales, and remains one of the best-selling and most influential artists in the history of popular    <script>
    wbq.push(function manageSearchScreen() {
  var $search = $('.js__search-screen');
  var $searchCloseBtn = $('#search-screen-close-btn');
  var $searchToggleBtn = $('.js__btn--search-toggle');
  var $mastheadSearchOpenBtn = $('#masthead-search-open-btn');
  var $nav = $('.js__nav');

  function lockSearchFocus() {
    $searchCloseBtn.focus();
    document.addEventListener('focusin', focusSearchCloseBtn);
  }

  function focusSearchCloseBtn(event) {
    if (!$.contains(document.getElementById('search-screen'), event.target)) {
      $searchCloseBtn.focus();
    }
  }

  function unlockSearchFocus() {
    document.removeEventListener('focusin', focusSearchCloseBtn);
    $mastheadSearchOpenBtn.focus();
  }

  // close X used to dismiss mobile search overlay
  $searchToggleBtn.click(function (event) {
    // Toggle search screen visibility
    $search.toggleClass('search-screen--is-open');

    if ($search.hasClass('search-screen--is-open')) {
      if (window.DEVICE_VIEW === 'desktop') {
        lockSearchFocus();
      }
      window.TMZ.utils.setAccessibilityFocusTrap('search-screen');
      $search.css('visibility', 'visible');
      setTimeout(function() {
        $nav.css('visibility', 'hidden');
      }, 300);
    } else {
      window.TMZ.utils.removeAccessibilityFocusTrap();
      if (window.DEVICE_VIEW === 'desktop') {
        unlockSearchFocus();
        $mastheadSearchOpenBtn.focus();
      }
      setTimeout(function() {
        $search.css('visibility', 'hidden');
      }, 300);
    }

    // Hide nav
    if ($nav.hasClass('nav--is-open')) {
      setTimeout(function () {
        $nav.removeClass('nav--is-open');
      }, 300);
    }
    event.preventDefault();
  });
});
   </script>

  <script id="newsletter-subscription-success" type="text">
   <p class="thanks">Thank you!<br> You have successfully signed up.</p>
  </script>
  <script>
   wbq.push(function renderSubscribeToNewsletterModal() {
    function renderThankYou() {
      document.getElementById('newsletter-subscription-form').innerHTML = document.getElementById('newsletter-subscription-success').innerHTML;
      window.TMZ.dispatch(window.TMZ.actions.destroyComponent('newsletter-subscription-lightbox-root', true));
    }

    function renderComponent(e) {
      e.preventDefault();
      e.stopPropagation();
      var lightboxDiv = document.createElement('div');
      var lightboxDivId = 'newsletter-subscription-lightbox-root';
      lightboxDiv.setAttribute('id', lightboxDivId);
      document.getElementById('lightbox-root').prepend(lightboxDiv);
      if (window.TMZ.utils.isValidEmail($('#newsletter-subscription-email').val())) {
        window.TMZ.renderComponent(
          'newsletter-subscription-lightbox-root',
          'newsletter-subscription-lightbox',
          {
            email: $('#newsletter-subscription-email').val(),
            id: 'newsletter-subscription-lightbox-root',
          },
        );
        document.addEventListener(window.TMZ.constants.actionTypes.SUBSCRIBE_TO_NEWSLETTER_ACCEPTED, renderThankYou);
      } else {
        alert('Please enter a valid email.');
      }
    }

    $('#newsletter-subscription-form').on('submit', renderComponent);
  });
  </script>
